% maxwidth is the original width if it is less than linewidth
% otherwise use linewidth (to make sure the graphics do not exceed the margin)
\makeatletter
\def\maxwidth{ %
  \ifdim\Gin@nat@width>\linewidth
    \linewidth
  \else
    \Gin@nat@width
  \fi
}
\makeatother

\definecolor{fgcolor}{rgb}{0.345, 0.345, 0.345}
\newcommand{\hlnum}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.686,0.059,0.569}{#1}}%
\newcommand{\hlstr}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.192,0.494,0.8}{#1}}%
\newcommand{\hlcom}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.678,0.584,0.686}{\textit{#1}}}%
\newcommand{\hlopt}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0,0,0}{#1}}%
\newcommand{\hlstd}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.345,0.345,0.345}{#1}}%
\newcommand{\hlkwa}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.161,0.373,0.58}{\textbf{#1}}}%
\newcommand{\hlkwb}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.69,0.353,0.396}{#1}}%
\newcommand{\hlkwc}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.333,0.667,0.333}{#1}}%
\newcommand{\hlkwd}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.737,0.353,0.396}{\textbf{#1}}}%
\let\hlipl\hlkwb

\usepackage{framed}
\makeatletter
\newenvironment{kframe}{%
 \def\at@end@of@kframe{}%
 \ifinner\ifhmode%
  \def\at@end@of@kframe{\end{minipage}}%
  \begin{minipage}{\columnwidth}%
 \fi\fi%
 \def\FrameCommand##1{\hskip\@totalleftmargin \hskip-\fboxsep
 \colorbox{shadecolor}{##1}\hskip-\fboxsep
     % There is no \\@totalrightmargin, so:
     \hskip-\linewidth \hskip-\@totalleftmargin \hskip\columnwidth}%
 \MakeFramed {\advance\hsize-\width
   \@totalleftmargin\z@ \linewidth\hsize
   \@setminipage}}%
 {\par\unskip\endMakeFramed%
 \at@end@of@kframe}
\makeatother

\definecolor{shadecolor}{rgb}{.97, .97, .97}
\definecolor{messagecolor}{rgb}{0, 0, 0}
\definecolor{warningcolor}{rgb}{1, 0, 1}
\definecolor{errorcolor}{rgb}{1, 0, 0}
\newenvironment{knitrout}{}{} % an empty environment to be redefined in TeX

\usepackage{alltt}

\usepackage{xcolor}
\usepackage{graphicx, tikz}



\newlength{\cardwidthspace}
\newlength{\cardheightspace}
\newlength{\cardmargin}
\setlength{\cardmargin}{0pt}% default => two side printing <<<<<<<<<<<<<<<

\setlength{\cardwidthspace}{18pt} % add right horizontal space
\setlength{\cardheightspace}{20pt}% add upper vertical space

% \setlength{\cardmargin}{\cardwidthspace}  % use for one side printing <<<<<<<<<<<<<<<           

\usepackage{etoolbox}   % for the patch 
\patchcmd{\card}
{\front\noindent\begin{picture}(0,0)}
{\front\noindent\begin{picture}(0,0)\advance\cardwidth by -\cardwidthspace\relax\advance\cardheight by -\cardheightspace\relax}
{}{}

\patchcmd{\card}
{\back\noindent\begin{picture}(0,0)}
{\back\noindent\begin{picture}(0,0)%
        \advance\cardwidth by -\cardwidthspace\relax%
        \advance\cardheight by -\cardheightspace\relax%
        \advance\@tempdimb by \cardmargin\relax% 
    }
{}{}

\renewcommand{\cardtextstylef}{\ttfamily \bfseries \large}
\renewcommand{\cardtextstyleb}{\ttfamily \bfseries \large}

\newcommand{\flashcard}[1]{% create new command for cards with blanks
    \card{% call the original \card command with twice the same argument (#1)
        \let\blank\frontcard% but let \blank behave like \frontcard the first time
        #1
    }{%
        \let\blank\backcard% and like \backcard the second time
        #1
    }%
}

\renewcommand{\flhead}{\vskip5pt \fboxsep=0pt {\small\bfseries\footnotesize Sagnorð | 动词}}
\renewcommand{\fcfoot}{\vskip5pt \fboxsep=0pt \hspace{2pt}{\small\bfseries\footnotesize 1K}}

\renewcommand{\blhead}{\vskip5pt {\small\bfseries\footnotesize Sagnorð | 动词 }}
\renewcommand{\bcfoot}{\vskip5pt \hspace{2pt}{\small\bfseries\footnotesize 1K}}


%% card templates
\card{\Large{vera} \normalsize{\textsubscript{(\textit{v.})}} \\ [2ex]
{Hundurinn \textcolor{red}{\underline{er}} svartur. }} 
{vera \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{v.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side
\textphonetic{[vɛːra]} \\
zh.: \emph{（be动词）是，就是} \\  [2ex]
\renewcommand*{\arraystretch}{0.8}
\begin{tabular}{p{1cm}l}
\textsc{1sg}: & er -- var -- verið \\ 
\textsc{2sg}: & ert -- varst -- verið \\ 
\textsc{3sg}: & er -- var -- verið \\ 
\end{tabular}
}

%% card templates
\card{\Large{eiga} \normalsize{\textsubscript{(\textit{v.})}} \\ [2ex]
{Þau \textcolor{red}{\underline{eiga}} fallegt hús. }} 
{eiga \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{v.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side
\textphonetic{[eiːɣa]} \\
zh.: \emph{拥有；有；应该} \\  [2ex]
\renewcommand*{\arraystretch}{0.8}
\begin{tabular}{p{1cm}l}
\textsc{1sg}: & á -- átti -- átt \\ 
\textsc{2sg}: & átt -- áttir -- átt \\ 
\textsc{3sg}: & á -- átti -- átt \\ 
\end{tabular}
}

\renewcommand{\bcfoot}{\vskip5pt \hspace{2pt}{\small\bfseries\footnotesize 1K}}


%% card templates
\card{\Large{land} \normalsize{\textsubscript{(\textit{n.})}} \\ [2ex]
{Fjölskyldan fór hringinn í kringum \textcolor{red}{\underline{landið}} . }}
{land \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{n.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side
\textphonetic{[lant]} \\
zh.: \emph{土地；国家；财产} \\  [2ex]
\renewcommand*{\arraystretch}{0.8}
\resizebox{.8\cardwidth}{!}{
\begin{tabular}{l l}
\textsc{sg}: & (frá) landi -- (til) lands \\ 
\textsc{pl}: & (frá) löndum -- (til) landa \\
\end{tabular}}
}

%% card templates
\card{\Large{ræða} \normalsize{\textsubscript{(\textit{v.})}} \\ [2ex]
{Við \textcolor{red}{\underline{ræðum}} efnið á morgun. }} 
{ræða \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{v.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side
\textphonetic{[raiːða]} \\
zh.: \emph{说话，讨论} \\  [2ex]
\renewcommand*{\arraystretch}{0.8}
\begin{tabular}{p{1cm}l}
\textsc{1sg}: & ræði -- ræddi -- rætt \\ 
\textsc{2sg}: & ræðir -- ræddir -- rætt \\ 
\textsc{3sg}: & ræðir -- ræddi -- rætt \\ 
\end{tabular}
}

\renewcommand{\fcfoot}{\vskip5pt \fboxsep=0pt \hspace{2pt}{\small\bfseries\footnotesize 1K}}

\renewcommand{\blhead}{\vskip5pt {\small\bfseries\footnotesize Sagnorð | 动词 }}
\renewcommand{\bcfoot}{\vskip5pt \hspace{2pt}{\small\bfseries\footnotesize 1K}}


%% card templates
\card{\Large{fylgja} \normalsize{\textsubscript{(\textit{v.})}} \\ [2ex]
{Hann \textcolor{red}{\underline{fylgir}} barninu í skólann. }} 
{fylgja \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{v.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side
\textphonetic{[fɪlca]} \\
zh.: \emph{跟随；陪伴} \\  [2ex]
\renewcommand*{\arraystretch}{0.8}
\begin{tabular}{p{1cm}l}
\textsc{1sg}: & fylgi -- fylgdi -- fylgt \\ 
\textsc{2sg}: & fylgir -- fylgdir -- fylgt \\ 
\textsc{3sg}: & fylgir -- fylgdi -- fylgt \\ 
\end{tabular}
}

\renewcommand{\fcfoot}{\vskip5pt \fboxsep=0pt \hspace{2pt}{\small\bfseries\footnotesize 1K}}

\renewcommand{\blhead}{\vskip5pt {\small\bfseries\footnotesize Lýsingarorð | 形容词 }}
\renewcommand{\bcfoot}{\vskip5pt \hspace{2pt}{\small\bfseries\footnotesize 1K}}


%% card templates
\card{\Large{fyrri} \normalsize{\textsubscript{(\textit{adj.})}} \\ [2ex]
{ \textcolor{red}{\underline{Fyrra}} svarið er rétt. }}
{fyrri \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{adj.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side
\textphonetic{[fɪrɪ]} \\
zh.: \emph{以前的} \\  [2ex]
\renewcommand*{\arraystretch}{0.8}
\resizebox{.8\cardwidth}{!}{
\begin{tabular}{ll}
\textsc{pos}: & fyrri  -- \\ 
\textsc{comp}: & fyrri -- fyrri -- fyrra \\ 
\textsc{superl}: &  \\
\end{tabular}}
}

{svið \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{n.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side

\begin{tabular}{l l}
\textsc{sg}: & (frá) sviði -- (til) sviðs \\ 
\textsc{pl}: & (frá) sviðum -- (til) sviða \\
\end{tabular}}
}

\renewcommand{\fcfoot}{\vskip5pt \fboxsep=0pt \hspace{2pt}{\small\bfseries\footnotesize 1K}}

\renewcommand{\blhead}{\vskip5pt {\small\bfseries\footnotesize Nafnorð | 名词 }}
\renewcommand{\bcfoot}{\vskip5pt \hspace{2pt}{\small\bfseries\footnotesize 1K}}


%% card templates
\card{\Large{nemandi} \normalsize{\textsubscript{(\textit{m.})}} \\ [2ex]
{Hann er ekki \textcolor{red}{\underline{nemandi}} í skólanum. }}
{nemandi \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{m.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side
\textphonetic{[nɛːmantɪ]} \\
zh.: \emph{学生} \\  [2ex]
\renewcommand*{\arraystretch}{0.8}
\resizebox{.8\cardwidth}{!}{
\begin{tabular}{l l}
\textsc{sg}: & (frá) nemanda -- (til) nemanda \\ 
\textsc{pl}: & (frá) nemendum -- (til) nemenda \\
\end{tabular}}
}

%% card templates

{stig \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{n.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side

\begin{tabular}{l l}
\textsc{sg}: & (frá) stigi -- (til) stigs \\ 
\textsc{pl}: & (frá) stigum -- (til) stiga \\
\end{tabular}}
}

\renewcommand{\fcfoot}{\vskip5pt \fboxsep=0pt \hspace{2pt}{\small\bfseries\footnotesize 1K}}

\renewcommand{\blhead}{\vskip5pt {\small\bfseries\footnotesize Atviksorð | 副词 }}
\renewcommand{\bcfoot}{\vskip5pt \hspace{2pt}{\small\bfseries\footnotesize 1K}}


%% card templates
\card{\Large{hingað} \normalsize{\textsubscript{(\textit{adv.})}} \\ [2ex]
{Komdu \textcolor{red}{\underline{hingað}} til mín. }}
{hingað \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{adv.})}} \\[1ex]
\textphonetic{[hiŋkað]} \\
zh.: \emph{从...到这里} \\  [2ex]
hingað (Indeclinable)}

\renewcommand{\bcfoot}{\vskip5pt \hspace{2pt}{\small\bfseries\footnotesize 1K}}


%% card templates
\card{\Large{bróðir} \normalsize{\textsubscript{(\textit{m.})}} \\ [2ex]
{ \textcolor{red}{\underline{Bróðir}} hennar er eldri en hún. }}
{bróðir \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{m.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side
\textphonetic{[prouːðɪr]} \\
zh.: \emph{兄弟} \\  [2ex]
\renewcommand*{\arraystretch}{0.8}
\resizebox{.8\cardwidth}{!}{
\begin{tabular}{l l}
\textsc{sg}: & (frá) bróður -- (til) bróður \\ 
\textsc{pl}: & (frá) bræðrum -- (til) bræðra \\
\end{tabular}}
}

{bygging \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{f.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side

\end{tabular}}

%% card templates
\card{\Large{vona} \normalsize{\textsubscript{(\textit{v.})}} \\ [2ex]
{Hann \textcolor{red}{\underline{vonast}} til að Persónuvernd endurskoði afstöðu sína. }} 
{vona \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{v.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side
\textphonetic{[vɔːna]} \\
zh.: \emph{希望} \\  [2ex]

\begin{tabular}{p{1cm}l}
\textsc{1sg}: & vona -- vonaði -- vonað \\ 
\textsc{2sg}: & vonar -- vonaðir -- vonað \\ 
\textsc{3sg}: & vonar -- vonaði -- vonað \\ 
\end{tabular}
}

%% card templates
\card{\Large{net} \normalsize{\textsubscript{(\textit{n.})}} \\ [2ex]
{Kosningarnar standa í tvær vikur og fara fram í gegnum \textcolor{red}{\underline{netið}} . }}
{net \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{n.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side
\textphonetic{[nɛːt]} \\
zh.: \emph{网；网络；互联网} \\  [2ex]

\begin{tabular}{l l}
\textsc{sg}: & (frá) neti -- (til) nets \\

\end{tabular}}
}

{atburður \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{m.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side

\textsc{pl}: & (frá) atburðum -- (til) atburða \\
\end{tabular}}
}

\renewcommand{\fcfoot}{\vskip5pt \fboxsep=0pt \hspace{2pt}{\small\bfseries\footnotesize 1K}}

\renewcommand{\blhead}{\vskip5pt {\small\bfseries\footnotesize Sagnorð | 动词 }}
\renewcommand{\bcfoot}{\vskip5pt \hspace{2pt}{\small\bfseries\footnotesize 1K}}


%% card templates
\card{\Large{viðurkenna} \normalsize{\textsubscript{(\textit{v.})}} \\ [2ex]
{Hann \textcolor{red}{\underline{viðurkennir}} að margir stjórnendur munu missa vinnuna. }} 
{viðurkenna \small{\textsubscript{(\textit{v.})}} \\[1ex] %% back side
\textphonetic{[vɪːðʏr̥cʰɛna]} \\
zh.: \emph{承认；认出} \\  [2ex]
\renewcommand*{\arraystretch}{0.8}
\begin{tabular}{p{1cm}l}
\textsc{1sg}: & viðurkenni -- viðurkenndi -- viðurkennt \\ 
\textsc{2sg}: & viðurkennir -- viðurkenndir -- viðurkennt \\ 
\textsc{3sg}: & viðurkennir -- viðurkenndi -- viðurkennt \\ 
\end{tabular}
}
